### **Chapter 8: POD vs. Physical**

**54:30**

**54 minutes, 30 seconds**

**content, using Tik Tok shop affiliates, GMAX ads, all that fun stuff. Let's first cover the different types of the archetypes of products that you can sell**

**54:38**

**54 minutes, 38 seconds**

**on Tik Tok shop. So, I kind of want to break it down into two sections. Of course, we could go down a rabbit hole and break it down even more, but really if you keep it really simple, there are**

**54:46**

**54 minutes, 46 seconds**

**two different archetypes and different avenues that you can go down on tactile shop. Number one is print on demand, right? These are these are items that**

**54:54**

**54 minutes, 54 seconds**

**are produced only when a customer places an order. No upfront costs and inventory. You pay per unit as orders come in. Lower profit margins because**

**55:02**

**55 minutes, 2 seconds**

**they pay for that. You pay for that convenience that happens. No storage or warehousing needed because they do it all for you. And easier to make an offer**

**55:09**

**55 minutes, 9 seconds**

**on products. Proc time equals faster, right? Uh, great for testing products with low volume. It's really speedy and you can get things up and running fast**

**55:16**

**55 minutes, 16 seconds**

**and zero risk, right? So, basically a print on demand product is a product where you use a middleman to do all the fulfillment for you. For example,**

**55:24**

**55 minutes, 24 seconds**

**Printify, which we'll be talking about here in a second, Printify is my ondemand supplier. So, when I'm selling a product on Tik Tok shop, Printify gets**

**55:31**

**55 minutes, 31 seconds**

**notified of my order and makes my product on demand, meaning only when that order gets processed and sends it directly to my customer, right? And this**

**55:40**

**55 minutes, 40 seconds**

**is an entire avenue of how print on demand works, right? Your print on demand store is connected to your Tik Tok shop. Your orders receive on Tik Tok. Print on demand starts producing**

**55:47**

**55 minutes, 47 seconds**

**that product and ships it directly to your customer. Tik Tok pays you out a couple weeks later and you pay Printify for the production of those products, right? And the difference is your profit**

**55:55**

**55 minutes, 55 seconds**

**margin. Now on the other side, what's called a physical product is bulk inventory purchasing, right? So you purchase a large quantity of product upfront before any sales have come in.**

**56:05**

**56 minutes, 5 seconds**

**Right? With print on demand, it's kind of subset of drop shipping where you only pay when you have a product produced, right? This is where you're paying upfront before the sale actually**

**56:14**

**56 minutes, 14 seconds**

**comes in. So, there's a higher upfront cost absolutely because you're playing placing bulk inventory. Uh significantly lower cost per unit cuz you are buying**

**56:22**

**56 minutes, 22 seconds**

**in bulk. They're going to give you discounts when it comes to the quantity that you're getting. Higher profit margins per sale. That's therefore, right? And require storage space. So,**

**56:30**

**56 minutes, 30 seconds**

**either you're shipping yourself, either you're using a 3PL or you're using FBT.**

**56:33**

**56 minutes, 33 seconds**

**You control fulfillment speed, which is quite nice. Risk of unsold inventory.**

**56:37**

**56 minutes, 37 seconds**

**This is the biggest risk that you do entail is that you've bought all this inventory that's worth something, but it's only worth something once it's cashed out, right? So, you risk of**

**56:45**

**56 minutes, 45 seconds**

**unsold sitting unsold inventory inside your place or your warehouse for your 3PL. This is better for established brands, of course, or more experienced**

**56:52**

**56 minutes, 52 seconds**

**seller that you know how to sell, you know what products you're going to be selling, you have a great team on your team for content. That's kind of where I see physical products doing the best.**

**57:00**

**57 minutes**

**Typically what we see inside of our inner circle is that we work with print on demand at the very beginning. We learn how Tik Tok shop operates, how to create content using affiliates, how the**

**57:08**

**57 minutes, 8 seconds**

**ecosystem works and what sells. And after stacking your first 10, 15, $20,000 in profit, which should only take a couple months to do so, take that**

**57:15**

**57 minutes, 15 seconds**

**print on demand store and income and the profit that you made and roll it into a physical product, an actual brand on Tik Tok shop. There's a little bit more**

**57:22**

**57 minutes, 22 seconds**

**long-term scalability within it. Right now, with print on demand, one thing that's so incredibly powerful about and why we always recommend it to first beginners is that there's no upfront**

**57:31**

**57 minutes, 31 seconds**

**capital to get started. It's literally impossible for you to lose money on print on demand as long as you don't do anything anything crazy or stupid, right? It's literally impossible to lose**

**57:40**

**57 minutes, 40 seconds**

**money. And that's why we always recommend it to someone who's starting off inside Tik Tok shop. You only pay when you get orders that are processed in. So, those orders are already**

**57:48**

**57 minutes, 48 seconds**

**guaranteed. The money is already coming into your account. So, you just not have to make the production to send it off.**

**57:53**

**57 minutes, 53 seconds**

**One thing that is a downside of print on demand that we're going to talk about later, cash flow is a big thing. Great problems to have when you're getting a lot of sales, but make sure you have some cash flow. I always recommend**

**58:01**

**58 minutes, 1 second**

**having $1,000 saved up to keep up with production costs. Uh with physical product, of course, I would recommend at least $5 to $10,000 to invest in physical inventory. The more the better.**

**58:11**

**58 minutes, 11 seconds**

**You're going to be able to play with a lot of wiggle room when it comes to your budget, especially on marketing and shipping and working with fulfillment providers that are going to be very speedy. But yeah, let's go into the**

**58:19**

**58 minutes, 19 seconds**

**steps that if we just had to break it down very simply of how Tik Tok shop operates and the step system that you would approach. This is this eight-step**

### **Chapter 16: GMV Max Ads**

**5:12:46**

**5 hours, 12 minutes, 46 seconds**

**Okay, let's dive into what GMV Max ads actually are. So, what is GMVAX? It's Tik Tok shops performance max style**

**5:12:53**

**5 hours, 12 minutes, 53 seconds**

**campaign of an ad platform where you give Tik Tok shops GMV Max three different things. a product, a daily budget, and a target ROI. And takes**

**5:13:01**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 1 second**

**everything else from there. It takes over the creative, the audience, the placements, the bidding, which ones are converting the best, which ones aren't converting best when it comes to cutting those and pushing more spend to the ones**

**5:13:09**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 9 seconds**

**that are doing well, right? This is not to be confused with what GMV stands for, right? Gross merchandise value. GMV Max is just how do they maximize that**

**5:13:17**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 17 seconds**

**revenue, right? It's a performance style campaign. So, that's really, really important to understand. So, let's actually dive into what this actually looks like, right? So, you give a budget**

**5:13:24**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 24 seconds**

**to Tik Tok. This could be $50. It could be a $100, whatever you give it to the G&B Max campaign, it'll take that budget and look at all the videos that we have**

**5:13:32**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 32 seconds**

**in circulation. It might be videos that we made ourselves under our own in-house account. That might be affiliate videos that were made on affiliate pages. That**

**5:13:40**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 40 seconds**

**might also be the shop tab on Tik Tok shop as well. And it'll go through a learning phase with all these different pieces of content, right? It'll learn which ones are converting the best,**

**5:13:48**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 48 seconds**

**which ones are making the most money for you actually converting. And we'll typically take about a penny and spend it into all these different avenues, right? That's kind of what it'll do.**

**5:13:55**

**5 hours, 13 minutes, 55 seconds**

**take a little penny, spend all these different places to go through the learning phase and see if it's actually creating conversions. And the ones that don't, they will cut those videos,**

**5:14:03**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 3 seconds**

**right? The ones that do, they'll continue adding spend to it, right?**

**5:14:06**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 6 seconds**

**Adding more spend, scaling that certain creative up, adding more budget and spend to the ones that are converting to you and cutting the ones that don't, like I kind of mentioned, right? And the**

**5:14:14**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 14 seconds**

**idea is that Tik Tok makes you profitable and keep spending money on the videos that convert the best. That's the idea of GMBB Max. It's entire idea**

**5:14:21**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 21 seconds**

**is it's a hands-off approach to running ads, right? It's best for especially for beginners who have never run ads before and it's easy system for passive income**

**5:14:29**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 29 seconds**

**from Tik Tok shop. Now, a couple things are a little bit of the negatives. I'm just going to give you guys a little heads up. One thing that is kind of annoying about GMBB Max is that it**

**5:14:37**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 37 seconds**

**combines paid growth and organic sales all in its calculation, right? So you might have a video going viral from a video that you made, right? Going viral**

**5:14:46**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 46 seconds**

**and it might get a million views and then GMVAX will kind of go below it and keep spending and keep growing and scaling it and it'll say inside your ROI**

**5:14:54**

**5 hours, 14 minutes, 54 seconds**

**that that is what did it right. GVM Max actually pushed that video. It's actually creating views and it was actually creating conversions when organically it was already doing it. So**

**5:15:02**

**5 hours, 15 minutes, 2 seconds**

**that's one of the downsides of it. it's kind of miscon skewed and actually not real like authentic data because it pulls organic and paid sales together.**

**5:15:11**

**5 hours, 15 minutes, 11 seconds**

**Just one thing to keep in mind. So, it's a very hands-off approach which for beginner sellers is awesome. For more advanced media buyers and people who run**

**5:15:18**

**5 hours, 15 minutes, 18 seconds**
